Major Textile Strike in the United States 73

Final Mediation Completely Fails; One Million Workers Take Direct Action; Most of More Than Three Thousand Factories Shut Down

(Washington) The most significant strike in American history began at 11:30 tonight. 850,000 textile workers across the country have gone on strike demanding shorter hours and higher wages. The National Labor Relations Board made a final effort to mediate, but it was completely ineffective. Only the week is Labor Day, and factories are closed as usual. Therefore, tonight's strike is only a nominal start. The truly dangerous period will be Tuesday. Some factories will remain open, and workers who oppose the strike will continue to work. However, most of the 3,370 factories across the country will be ordered to close by the factory owners. According to Gorman, the vice president of the American Textile Workers Union, the strike will be fully supported. President Roosevelt is also paying close attention, but has no plans to intervene. Sloan, the president of the Yarn Industry Association, is now in New York, saying that the treatment of workers in the yarn industry has increased by 70% compared to 1929. Since the total number of workers has increased by 140,000, working hours have also been reduced to 40 hours per week. The National Labor Relations Board is now working hard to maintain peace in other industries and stipulates that wherever a majority of workers have formed a union, those workers can represent the entire body and negotiate with the owners. After the publication of this regulation, it should reduce the strike movement, because employers often have disputes over the issue of recognizing the union. The American Federation of Labor believes that this regulation is a great victory for labor. (1st National News Dispatch)

Textile Industry Announces Strike Affecting One Million People 74

Silk Factories Also Receive Strike Notice

(New York) The general textile strike notice was issued at 11:00 tonight. At least one million people are directly or indirectly affected by the workers. 200,000 workers in silk factories and rayon factories also received notice today to join the strike. Although the director of the National Labor Mediation Board claimed yesterday afternoon that the labor unrest could still be salvaged, all hopes of mediation were completely extinguished last night. After a meeting of the board of directors of the American Textile Workers Union, strike committee chairman Gorman stated at night that the situation had not changed and the strike decision was implemented. It is now expected that 15,000 woolen workers in New Jersey, Pennsylvania, and New England, 500,000 workers in 1,200 yarn factories across the country, 200,000 workers in the silk and rayon industries, and 250,000 workers in the cotton clothing industry will join the strike. Union leaders are confident that they can force textile employers to accept their demands. The demands of the American Textile Workers Union are as follows: ㈠ Work five days a week, six hours a day, with uniform wages everywhere; ㈡ Existing weekly wages shall not be reduced; ㈢ End discrimination against union workers; ㈣ Reduce piecework; ㈤ Recognize the union as an agency for worker negotiation; ㈥ Establish an arbitration board; ㈦ Increase the participation of the National Recovery Administration in local labor bureaus. The employers, on the other hand, claim that reduced working hours will increase production costs, which is difficult to bear. A worker's strike is tantamount to encouraging the use of force and riots as tools for creating legal amendments and industry regulations for the recovery. From the employers' point of view, this is unacceptable. (1st Reuters Dispatch)

(New York) The general strike in the weaving industry will be implemented tonight at 11 o'clock. 900,000 people will join the strike in the north, south, and along the Atlantic coast, including 500,000 in the cotton weaving industry and 200,000 each in the wool and silk industries. Although Washington-related parties still express some optimism, hoping that a compromise can still be reached at the last moment, the general feeling is that the strike is inevitable, because Garrison, the director of the National Labor Relations Adjustment Bureau, has tried his best to mediate, but the employer's attitude is still unyielding. Strike leaders hope that all 900,000 people will be able to join the strike, but according to the employer's estimate, only 15% will participate, and the factories will still open as usual tomorrow. It is said that among the 900,000 workers, there are still a large number of unemployed workers, so it is impossible to predict how many will participate in the strike. Gorman, the leader of the strike committee, recently sent a telegram to the president of the American Veterans of the European War Association and the president of the Foreign Veterans of the War Association, saying that there are quite a few veterans who are related to the strike's goals, and that this strike movement is not the same as the Communist Party's attempt to create incidents. Please provide spiritual assistance to the strike. It is estimated that after the strike is realized, the situation will be quite peaceful. The only thing to fear is that the factories may hire people who specialize in destroying strikes to resist the strikers, which may cause retaliatory behavior by the strikers. (1st Havas Dispatch)

China Contacts the United States Regarding Silver Policy 75

(Washington) Political and financial experts here today stated that the Chinese government is now exploring the silver policy of the United States in order to cope with it. The Chinese government is eager to cooperate internationally in stabilizing silver prices. The steps taken by China to explore American policy are roughly as follows: First, the State Department has received a Chinese request for an explanation of President Roosevelt's monetary policy. Second, Li Ming, the chairman of the Bank of China, is meeting with leaders in the New York banking and financial circles and plans to come here to meet with Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi. Third, President's monetary policy advisor Professor Rogers will soon return to the United States after inspecting the silver situation in China. Fourth, the Chinese Embassy here is paying close attention to the US government's monetary actions. Today, unconfirmed news is circulating in diplomatic circles that President Roosevelt plans to discuss the silver issue with China, the United Kingdom, Japan, France, and Italy, but the government says it knows nothing about it. Financial circles believe that the President will take a conservative policy on silver for the time being. As for the above-mentioned request from the Chinese government to the State Department, officialdom is unwilling to disclose it, but it is understood that in addition to requesting an explanation of the President's silver policy, it also stated that the London Silver Agreement was concluded to stabilize silver prices. Now, the US government is implementing the Silver Act passed by Congress, which is preventing silver prices from being stabilized. (1st National News Dispatch)

Forward Prospects of the Naval Conference: Japan's Proposal Affords Flexibility 78

Requesting a Change to the Gross Tonnage Principle, Prepared to Exert All Efforts in Negotiations with Britain and America

(Tokyo) The London Preliminary Conference is scheduled to commence negotiations in early November after Rear Admiral Yamamoto, the Japanese naval representative, arrives in England with the Japanese government's instructions. Since the announcement of the Japanese government's disarmament policy, various opinions have arisen in Europe and America, making the realization of the formal naval disarmament conference next year a matter of considerable concern. Japan's policy is based on the principle of excluding the current ratio system and adopting a gross tonnage system, while demanding substantial reductions in both quality and quantity. However, Britain and America's disarmament attitude, in terms of quality, is limited to 32,000 tons with 14-inch guns, and the United States is very insistent on adhering to the current ratio system. Therefore, the future of the formal conference is quite pessimistic. (2nd, Japan Associated Press)

(Tokyo) The Japanese government's fundamental policy for next year's disarmament conference and the instructions for the disarmament preparatory talks will be formally decided in the cabinet meeting this week and taken to London by Rear Admiral Isoroku Yamamoto. It is reported that the government's new disarmament strategy for the disarmament conference has the following two notable characteristics: ㈠ It is based on the government's absolute advocacy of naval disarmament, with ensuring substantial disarmament and international peace as the primary goal. ㈡ The content of this proposal is very flexible, making it possible for any country to accept it. Therefore, if Britain and America do not frankly accept this proposal, the government is determined to put forward a tough proposal, even if it leads to the breakdown of next year's conference. At the preparatory conference to be reopened in early October, this absolute principle will be presented, and all efforts will be exerted through individual and multilateral diplomatic negotiations to secure the understanding and approval of Britain and America. If the preparatory conference fails to achieve satisfactory results on this point and ends in failure, Japan will only conclude that next year's conference cannot be held in reality. (2nd, Domei News Agency)

Japan Uses Torture to Interrogate Railway Workers: Soviet Russia Protests to Japan 80

Female Secretary of the China Eastern Railway Headquarters Arrested, Fingers Clamped with Metal Rods, Water Poured into Mouth and Nose

(Moscow) The following TASS communiqué has been published here: [On August 31st, the Japanese Ambassador to the Soviet Union, Mr. Ota, visited the Deputy Commissar for Foreign Affairs, Mr. Stomonyakov. Mr. Stomonyakov immediately stated that, according to information received by the Foreign Affairs Committee, Ms. Golovina, a female secretary of the General Affairs Department of the China Eastern Railway, was arrested by the Japanese military police on August 22nd and imprisoned in the military police headquarters. After a while, Ms. Golovina was taken to another room for interrogation, during which she was subjected to extremely cruel and inhumane torture. Several metal rods were clamped between her fingers, and at the same time, her fingers were tightly pulled with ropes, causing Ms. Golovina to faint. During the interrogation, Ms. Golovina's head and face were repeatedly punched, her hair was torn apart, and water was poured into her mouth and nasal cavity. This kind of brutal torture was carried out by Japanese personnel.

On August 27th, Ms. Golovina's condition became critical, so she was led to the street and sent home in the first hired car that passed by, without any assistance. At the same time, she was warned that if her health recovered slightly, she would be arrested again. Currently, the Soviet Consulate General in Harbin has assisted in sending her to the hospital due to her critical condition.

Mr. Stomonyakov further stated that this accurate information was reported to the Soviet Consulate General in Harbin by Ms. Golovina herself, and it can also prove that the ominous news published in the newspapers about the arrested railway workers of the China Eastern Railway being subjected to torture is not false. The newspapers all reported that the arrested railway workers of the China Eastern Railway were subjected to torture in order to make them admit that they had directed attacks on the eastern section of the China Eastern Railway. However, whether in the past or present, these railway workers themselves and their families have always been the first to suffer in such attacks.

Mr. Stomonyakov, based on the instructions of the Soviet government, protested to Mr. Ota regarding this action by the Japanese authorities in Manchuria, and stated that the Soviet government sincerely hopes that the Japanese government will take decisive steps to stop the aforementioned unacceptable actions, as they are clearly detrimental to the relations between the two countries. (2nd, TASS)

The Current Situation in Turbulent Europe (Italian Dispatch) 91

Deteriorating Situation in Central Europe: Economic Decline in Italy

Italy is also a dissatisfied party to the Treaty of Versailles and is theoretically very close to Germany. However, there are still many differences between them. For example, Italy has never had ethnic problems domestically. The Fascists have never excluded Jews or other ethnic groups. The treatment is generally equal. Germany is not like that. In order to exclude Jews, the whole country is in turmoil, and even the world has a small shock. Germany itself is also greatly affected economically. Secondly, in terms of religion, Italy is of course the base camp of Catholicism, and Mussolini and his subordinates have not had conflicts with the Church. Germany, on the other hand, has a strong tendency to exclude the old religion with the new religion. Although this is not a fundamental opposition between Italy and Germany, it is indeed enough to affect their cooperation, at least calling her a little further away, adding a weight to the opposition of hegemony.

In mid-June, two dictators with a world-swallowing spirit, Mussolini and Hitler, had several earnest talks without the participation of a third person. So far, its content has not been fully disclosed, but this meeting is closely related to the Austrian independence issue, which no one denies. In Austria itself, Germany's current strategy is to merge with Germany, but after the merger of Germany and Austria, Italy and Germany will immediately enter a state of close combat, with no room for buffer. At the same time, Tyrol feels more threatened, and the whole of Italy is in anxiety. Just as the late Austrian Prime Minister Dollfuss firmly opposed the merger of Germany and Austria, Italy took the opportunity to advocate Austria's independence in order to establish hegemony in Central Europe.

In terms of geographical relations, historical habits, and the current economic situation of Austria, its independence cannot be maintained in the long run. It should be fully merged with Germany, and Italy needs to extend its economic power to Austria over the high mountains, violating the natural geographical separation. Germany is just the opposite, and it is easy to do so. It can also be extended to Hungary, which hinders Italy's establishment of hegemony in Central Europe. At the same time, it aroused the dissatisfaction of the Little Entente. France naturally raised the Treaty of Versailles as a weapon of confrontation. As a result, Italy became more powerful, and the power to contain Germany became greater. Little did they know that the Germans and the German people of Austria! The National Socialist Party! First, they launched an attack and killed the Austrian dictator Dollfuss.

The bullet of Sarajevo once stirred up the European War. Dollfuss was killed, and the Austrian Home Guard relied heavily on Italian support and tried its best to suppress the National Socialist Party. If Hitler had been more enthusiastic at that time and given more assistance to the Austrian National Socialist Party, then the situation in Austria would have been very chaotic, and it would have been difficult to guarantee that the riots would not affect Italy. It was expected that Italian troops would come to the border and interfere across the border. Then who can guarantee that there will be no World War II. Who knows that Hitler kept a calm attitude and never reached out to Austria, which did not cause a major change, and overcame a dangerous situation. It was also the economic breakdown of Europe, especially Germany, that made her dare not arbitrarily break into trouble and seek her own defeat.

Germany is indeed in extreme economic difficulty, but what about Italy? Now, the financial situation of Italy and the general economic situation are briefly described as follows:

The deterioration of Italy's finances did not start today, but this year is particularly bad. As of the end of May, the budget for this year was short of 68.03 million lira. When the budget was prepared before July last year, the assumed "deficit" was only 280 million lira. Little did they know that the difference was so huge. From July last year to May this year, the domestic public debt increased by 50.09 million lira in eleven months, and the total amount of debt increased from 972.15 million lira to 1,022.24 million lira. Even if the Italian government spends all its efforts to save government expenditures and increase taxes, its effectiveness is still very small. In the fiscal year 1934 to 1935, the fiscal budget is still short of more than 176 million lira. From the deterioration of the finances, we can get a glimpse of the decline of the national economy. Although she tried hard to use reciprocal trade agreements, control foreign exchange and credit, and implement a quota system, foreign trade imports increased by 4.6%, while exports decreased by 15%. The number of import surpluses increased from 62.9 million lira last year to 114.8 million lira this year. Italy's international balance of payments, in addition to trade, relies on the consumption of foreign tourists. Although this has increased considerably, it does not make up for the actual situation and only slightly provides funding. Moreover, the central bank's cash reserves have decreased by 600 million lira from the end of last year to June this year, which is a clear sign of capital flight. In such an economic situation, is it not a disguised suicide to fight a war? But we know that the European countries always use external development as a tool to suppress domestic panic. What's more, Italy is expanding upwards, and of course, it will expand its hegemony to cover up its ugliness. In the end, it can only firmly grasp Central Europe, extend to North Africa, and even use military force to do whatever it takes. This is the crisis in Europe and also the current cancer in the world. (August 8th, 2nd in Rome)

North Pan Flood Risk in Kaifeng 92

Kaifeng Dispatch, a few days ago, the dikes of the Second Dam of the Twentieth Fortress in North Pan, Kaifeng, overflowed, and the torrents rushed, posing a very dangerous situation. Chen Ruzhen, director of the River Affairs Bureau, and Zheng Kanghou, county magistrate of Kaifeng, and others, went to inspect the site on the morning of the 29th to supervise the rapid repair. Chen Zheng and others returned to Bian from Pan at around 5:00 PM today. According to the talks, from the fourth dam of the Nineteenth Fortress to the lower boundary of the Twentieth Fortress, the top of the dam is being scoured by large torrents, and many dikes have collapsed. New and old stone materials have been exhausted, and hemp bags are being used for emergency protection. However, the large torrents are still scouring and excavating, making it difficult to maintain for a long time. Moreover, heavy rain in Shaanxi and Gansu will cause large floods to arrive soon. It is difficult to guarantee safety without emergency preparations. It has been requested that the Mining Committee transport a large number of stone materials before September 5th. At the same time, the Lower North Branch Bureau is ordered to quickly transport black steel wire cages for workers to purchase old, bricks nearby, load them into cages, and throw them to protect them to provide emergency relief. More than 200 willow trees have been hung in the lower section of the 20th Fortress, but the soil work to reinforce the levee is extremely important. As soon as the special subsidy from the provincial government is allocated and the engineering fees from various counties in Kaifeng are paid, bids will be invited to rush to complete the work. Zhu Tang, the chief engineer of the Yellow Disaster Relief Association, also talked about the breach in Changyuan, and met with Lin Chengxiu, Hu Yuanhui, and Sun Qingze to agree on four measures: 1) encircle the willow dams to make them silt up; 2) build soil cabinets behind the willow dams to cut off the flow; 3) block the connecting ditches; 4) rush to build bank protection projects. As for the issue of responsibility, after the completion of the flood control project by the Engineering Relief Group last year, the central government sent personnel to inspect and accept it, considering it to be strong. The remaining flood control projects were all transferred to the Hebei Provincial River Affairs Bureau for acceptance and responsible management. The responsibility for the breach has been clearly established. (August 30th)

Wuhu Rice Merchants Request Relaxation of the Prohibition 93

Wuhu Dispatch, the Anhui Provincial Government, due to the severe drought in the province and to prevent panic among the people, has issued several clear orders prohibiting the export of rice. After the new rice is on the market, it will be allowed to circulate within the province. In order to prevent smuggling, it is stipulated that the special commissioner's offices in each district and the county governments are responsible for regulation, and the local public security bureaus are responsible for investigation. In southern Anhui, in prosperous years, the rice and grain gathered in Wuhu are transported out, reaching as many as 8 million shi per year. Those transported by sail from Hexian Yuxikou to other provinces also amount to millions of shi. Therefore, the authorities attach great importance to the above two places. Since the issuance of the prohibition order, rice merchants in the two places have continued to smuggle rice out, which has a great impact on the people's food supply. Therefore, the inspection is even stricter. Recently, more than 30,000 bags of smuggled rice have been seized in Yuxikou, and thousands of shi have also been seized in Wuhu. The Provincial Food Regulation Committee received a report and specially sent Commissioner Li Zhenya to Wuhu to handle the matter. After Li arrived in Wuhu, he repeatedly consulted with Commissioner Wang Hezai, Public Security Bureau Chief Yu Qiguang, and rice industry leaders of the Chamber of Commerce. After Chairman Li Dachu of the grain purchasing and transportation industry requested and after sending a telegram to the provincial government for instructions, it was approved to flexibly resell them within the province. The issue of seizing smuggled rice has come to an end. However, the rice merchants believe that Anhui Province's rice production, even in times of extreme drought, can still supply the people's food with a surplus. Even in the year of the great flood in the 20th year of the Republic of China, the disaster area cannot be said to be not vast, but Hefei Sanhe and other places still have millions of shi of surplus rice. Low grain prices hurt farmers, which is not without impact. Moreover, there are many provinces in the country where the supply of rice and grain is insufficient. If this surplus is not allowed to be exported, then the majority of rural areas in Anhui will never have hope of revival. Therefore, the Wuhu Chamber of Commerce and various rice industries have planned to send representatives to the province after Commissioner Li to present the advantages and disadvantages to the provincial authorities and request permission to relax the prohibition. It is rumored that the provincial government also does not insist on using the surplus rice to absorb a large amount of cash to regulate the rural areas and save various industries, but only after a detailed survey and statistics of the rice and grain in the province, if it does not affect the people's food supply in the province, can a decision be made on the policy. (1st)

It is Said that the Japanese-British Alliance and the Japanese-French Agreement are Unlikely to be Realized According to the Japanese Foreign Ministry 94

Japan Still Adheres to a Policy of Exclusive Control Over China

According to the Osaka Mainichi Newspaper on August 26th, following the reports from a Dutch journalist in Tokyo regarding a possible Japanese-British political agreement, there have recently been reports from French official circles in Shanghai about a possible Japanese-French political agreement. The Japanese Foreign Ministry believes that the possibility of these reports becoming reality is still weak. However, the rumors of a Japanese-British alliance and a Japanese-French agreement are related to all countries with interests in China, and they see the 1935 Customs Special Conference as a turning point, so the Foreign Ministry is quite concerned. Furthermore, the Foreign Ministry considers these rumors important in light of the recent British industrial mission's survey of Manchuria and the French consortium's investment in Manchuria. However, the fundamental policy of the Foreign Ministry regarding diplomacy towards China, which must be centered on Japan, concerning individual or multilateral political and economic agreements with third countries, has been decided as follows: 1. Japan's policy towards China, since withdrawing from the League of Nations, marks a new era. All political issues related to China will be resolved through direct negotiations between China and Japan, based on Japan's own views. This was communicated to various countries at the London Disarmament Preparatory Conference in late July. 2. The military and political issues recorded in the Anglo-Japanese Alliance treaty are relics of the past. Now, to ensure the autonomy of national defense, Japan is unwilling to be a watchdog for third countries in China. 3. If countries with interests in China can change their policy of hindering Japan's policy towards China, Japan is willing to support the principle of open door and equal opportunity in commerce in a passive and gentlemanly manner.

The Japanese are Actively Building the Najin Port in Northern Korea 95

In Peacetime, It Can Serve as a Base for Engulfing the Economy of Manchuria and Mongolia

In Wartime, the Port Can Undertake Important Military Missions

An Dong Dispatch: Since the completion of the three major ports in northern Korea, namely Chongjin and Unggi, the Japanese have controlled the authority of the economy of Manchuria and Mongolia, and achieved their goal of engulfing our Northeast. Recently, with the completion of the Kilhoe Railway, the importance of Najin Port has surpassed the other two ports. In the event of a major war in the Far East in the future, if Najin Port is completed step by step according to the Japanese plan, it will bear the same important military and transportation missions as Dalian. Moreover, the transportation network composed of the South Manchuria Railway from Dalian to Changchun, the Kilhoe Railway from Changchun to Najin, and other branch lines will provide a great boost to the port's handling capacity. Therefore, the Japanese are actively building it in stages, so as to complete it as soon as possible. The so-called policy of "three ports and five railways" for invading Manchuria and Mongolia has now been realized. Now, we explore the importance of Najin Port and its general outline, and record it clearly as follows:

Population Overview: Since the opening of the port, in less than a year and a half (nine months after the first phase of the port construction plan), the population has increased to more than 14,000, of which Koreans number more than 9,100, Japanese more than 2,800, and overseas Chinese 87, totaling 13,907.

Economic Construction: Since the opening of new shipping routes directly to Japan and Taiwan in April 1933, transportation has become extremely convenient. The shipping schedules of the ships are listed as follows:

Ship Name Port Name Shipping Company Frequency

Seikai Maru Niigata Port Hatoba Steamship Company Three times a month

Hokusei Maru Fushiki Port Hokuriku Steamship Company Once a month

Manshu Maru Tsuruga Port Kitanippon Steamship Company Three times a month

Wuchang Maru Osaka Osaka Shosen Kaisha Once a week

Guizhou Maru Osaka Osaka Shosen Kaisha Once a week

Two others Osaka Osaka Shosen Kaisha Once a week

In addition, the Korean Postal Steamship, Mitsui & Co., Manchuria Transportation and other companies also have ships sailing. The throughput is not yet considerable, only 5,000 tons per day, of which 80% are building materials and financial goods, and the rest are food and groceries. Most of the timber is supplied from Korea and Japan, and metals and other goods are mostly obtained from Osaka and Kobe. Rice is mostly imported from Wonsan and Busan, and vegetables are mostly imported from Xinjing. In the future, when Najin Port is completed, it can handle 9 million tons of cargo, and its development is truly immeasurable.

Future Commerce: Since the opening of Najin Port, large-scale construction has been carried out. It is estimated that in 1933, the consumption of timber, red pine, cedar, and larch was about 1.38 million cubic feet, logs were about 56,000 cubic feet, and American pine was about 15,000 cubic feet, with a total value of about 260,000 gold yuan. The activeness of the construction can be seen. Most of those who come to reside in Najin due to its prosperity are from the labor sector and Shandong. There are food stores and grocery stores of all kinds. Among the general population, there are 91 people engaged in the restaurant business, 605 carpenters, 585 transportation workers, 95 fishermen, and 443 farmers. Other businesses such as civil engineering contractors, silk stores, cafes, bookstores, and doctors are all available. In the future, after the completion of Najin Port, the prosperity of commerce will surely make it a large commercial port.

Japanese Institutions: The Japanese institutions established in Najin include the Najin Town Office, police station, Chamber of Commerce and Industry, Veterans Association branch, fire brigade, Medical Association, Timber Merchants Association, Civil Engineering and Construction Industry Cooperative Association, and other associations. The only financial institutions are the post office, the Unggi Mujin Company branch, and the Colonial Bank branch, of which the post office has become the main financial institution. This is one of the characteristics of Najin.

Dense Transportation Network: The Kilhoe Railway terminates at Najin Port, but the section below is not yet completed, only to Unggi. It is about 37 miles from Unggi to Najin, and is scheduled to be completed in July 1935. At that time, the first phase of the construction plan will also be completed. Currently, there are buses running from Najin to Unggi, making 15 round trips per day, and it takes 40 minutes to arrive. There are also buses from Najin to Outer Chongjin, making 5 round trips per day, taking 4 hours and 40 minutes. In addition, there are regular ships between Najin, Chongjin, and Unggi, with three ships scheduled every day. Judging from the current situation, transportation is already very convenient. In the future, when the Kilhoe Railway is completed, transportation will be even more convenient.

Port Construction Plan: The total cost of the Najin port construction budget is 64 million yuan. The first phase of the plan started in 1933 and is scheduled to be completed in 1937, with a construction cost of 25.5 million yuan. The northwest part of Najin Port will be specially filled in artificially, and three docks will be built, as well as a vehicle yard, warehouses, roads, and open storage areas, which can accommodate four 8,000-ton ships and eight 7,000-ton ships. The throughput capacity can reach 3 million tons. To the west of the city, a special freight car yard and engine house will be built. In terms of railways, it is imperative to complete the Unggi and Najin sections. After the completion of the first phase of the plan, agricultural products from the Jilin-Heilongjiang border area and special products from northern Manchuria can be exported through Najin. The second phase of the industrial cost is about 20 million yuan, and three wharves will be built with an annual cargo throughput of 3 million tons, which can accommodate eight 8,000-ton ships, sixteen 7,000-ton ships, and eight 4,000-ton ships. The third phase of the project costs about 20 million yuan, and it is planned to accommodate twelve 8,000-ton ships, twenty-four 7,000-ton ships, and twelve 4,000-ton ships within four years. The cargo throughput can be increased to 9 million tons, which can surpass Dalian. That is the period when Najin Port will be completely successful.

Zhou Column Captured Xingguo Laoyingpan 96

And Captured More Than 30 Pseudo-Instructors and Others

The Zhou Army Has Arrived Thirty Miles from Xingcheng

Nanchang Dispatch: The 囗 Column Zhou Hunyuan, leading the Xie Wanxiao and other divisions, is stationed in the middle of the Gan River, contacting the Western Route on the one hand to encircle and suppress the remnants of the Xiao bandits on the west bank of the Gan River, and attacking Xingguo from Taihe on the other hand. After clearing out the scattered bandits east of Shacai and west of Taihe, the column continued to attack Xingguo County. On August 13th, they arrived at Laoyingpan (west of Xingguo). The bandits had built strong fortifications on the front, and the high mountains and steep peaks were extremely dangerous. The pseudo-61st and 62nd Regiments, the pseudo-6th Division, and local scattered bandits resisted stubbornly. The column used aircraft and artillery to bombard the bandit fortifications, and the fortifications and trenches were completely destroyed. Then the infantry charged in, and within only two hours, Laoyingpan was completely recovered. The remnants of the bandits fled in disarray towards Chongxianwei and Gaoxingwei. Gaoxingwei is located twenty to thirty miles west of Xingguo County. In the 19th year of the Republic of China, the 19th Route Army annihilated more than 10,000 bandits here. The bandits retreated to Ruijin and Doushi to recuperate for half a year before deciding to turn from southern Jiangxi to eastern Jiangxi in the Second Pseudo-National Congress and join the bandits led by Fang Zhimin on the borders of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui. This led to the fourth and fifth encirclements and suppressions by the National Army. Now the Third and Sixth Route Armies are approaching Shicheng, Ningdu, and Xingguo. The Zhou Column is following up on the bandits towards Gaoxingwei, only thirty to forty miles from Xingguo City.

Zhou Hunyuan telegraphed on the 25th to report the battle situation. The telegram said: "Our column captured the important pass of Laoyingpan belonging to Xingguo on the first day of the month. The general situation is as follows: (A) The bandits on the front had solid fortifications and resisted desperately. Fortunately, our officers and soldiers fought bravely with the assistance of aircraft and artillery bombardment. After two hours of fierce fighting, the bandits were defeated and fled. Our army firmly occupied Laoyingpan and the surrounding heights. (B) The bandits resisting were the pseudo-61st and 62nd Regiments and the entire pseudo-6th Division. After being defeated, most of them fled in a disarray to Gaoxingwei, and a part fled to Chongxianwei. (C) In this battle, we captured more than 30 pseudo-regiment instructors and others, killed about 200 bandits, wounded twice as many, and captured many spoils." (September 1st)

Huangshan Park in Anhui is Scheduled to Open 97

The Wuhu-Tunxi Highway Has Been Completed

Wuhu Dispatch: Huangshan Mountain in Huizhou, Anhui Province, is a famous scenic spot in southern Anhui. In the past, due to the steep mountain roads, there were few visitors. Later, the local authorities of this province gathered important domestic figures and contemporary celebrities to form the Huangshan Construction Committee, and opened up the best areas of Huangshan Mountain as Huangshan Park. After half a year and spending huge sums of money, the park has now been arranged and is scheduled to open on September 15th, inviting important domestic figures and representatives from various places to participate in the celebration. Moreover, as Wuhu is a commercial port on the Yangtze River and the first town in Anhui, it has been expanding roads and building Zeshan Park in recent years, which is also nearing completion. At the same time, the city area will be guided for those arriving in Wuhu. The Wuhu-Tunxi Highway from Wuhu to Huangshan has been mostly completed and is connected to the Jingwu Highway. If you transfer from Wuhu to Xuancheng (to Xuancheng, the train is more convenient), the Director of the Construction Department, Liu Yiyan, recently specially hired Shao Yizhou, the President of Wuhan University of Technology, to go to Huangshan to prepare everything in advance. The mountain is divided into two parts, inside and outside the mountain. Outside the mountain, the roads are crisscrossing and lead in all directions. Inside the mountain, there are five scenic areas such as "Yingu" and "Tianhai", which are very convenient for sightseeing. (August 31st)

The Jiangsu Construction Department Formulates a Drought Relief Construction Plan 98

Allocates 4 Million Yuan in Water Conservancy Public Bonds

To Dredge Rivers in Various Counties South of the Yangtze River

Zhenjiang Dispatch: The drought this year in the counties south of the Yangtze River in Jiangsu Province is extremely severe. The Jiangsu Construction Department has specially formulated a drought relief construction plan, allocating 4 million yuan in water conservancy public bonds to dredge the rivers in various counties south of the Yangtze River as a remedial measure. The plan is extracted as follows:

(1) Dredging the Junhe River from Zhenjiang to Wujin and Regulating Lian Lake in Danyang. The Jiangnan Canal from Zhenjiang Jingkou, through Danyang to Wujin, is about 80 kilometers long. It is both an important transportation route and a hub for receiving and discharging river water. To its north are the Danzukou, Yuehe, Baogang, Menghe, Desheng Port, and Zaogang ports, which are closely connected with the tides of the Yangtze River. It is truly the main vein of the waterways in Jiangnan. Danyang originally had Lian Lake, which was a natural reservoir. It receives water from afar and is also the source of water for the canal section. In dry years, it can also store water to help nearby farmland. Recently, the gates have collapsed and their function has been lost. The regulation of water sources has lost an assistant. In addition, the gates at various ports connected to the Yangtze River have been abandoned, making it difficult to control them. The canal itself is also blocked by silt, which has led to the phenomenon of intermittent flow in winter and spring for a long time. Its treatment is really urgent. The Canal Discussion Association once had a plan to raise the water level by setting up gates. Although the project is more economical, this is a work-relief project, so it is necessary to focus on earthwork. Therefore, manual dredging is still the principle. The construction methods are as follows: (A) Junhe River (1) The scope of construction is to dredge the entire canal from Zhenjiang to Changzhou, which is 80 kilometers long, and to dredge the Danzu River and the Danyang Huanzhang River to smooth the flow of the river. It should dredge the Danzu River for 0.925 kilometers and the Danyang Huanzhang River for 4.160 kilometers. The total length of the construction line is 85.085 kilometers. (2) Dredging method: manual dredging is used for all. The longitudinal slope of the whole river is regulated to be parallel to the lowest ice level line in previous years, which is about one to 77030. The depth is uniformly dredged to one meter below the lowest water level line. The average width of the riverbed is 12 meters, and the bank slope is one to 1.25. A total of about 7 million cubic meters of soil needs to be excavated. (3) Budget: Each cubic meter of soil is priced at one corner, totaling about 700,000 yuan. Filling and water drainage is about 60,000 yuan, and management and reserve costs are about 40,000 yuan, totaling about 800,000 yuan. (B) Lian Lake: Restore the original reservoir, build five-hole Tongyun floodgates, each hole is 6 meters, and one sluice gate, about 80,000 yuan. Repairing the Zhiyun and Lian Lake culverts is about 30, totaling about 30,000 yuan. Repairing the Lian Lake Huangjin fill is 40 meters long, about 30,000 yuan. The embankment is 16 kilometers long, about 180,000 cubic meters of earth needs to be piled up, each cubic meter is one corner, about 18,000 yuan. Dredging the Lian Lake Tongyun ditch is 6 kilometers long, about 230,000 cubic meters of earth needs to be excavated, each cubic meter is one corner, about 23,000 yuan. Management reserve is about 19,000 yuan, totaling about 200,000 yuan. The above two projects of dredging and restoring Lian Lake total 1 million yuan, and the total earthwork is about 7.41 million cubic meters. If the work is calculated for three months, about 2.47 million cubic meters per month, that is, 82,000 cubic meters must be done every day. Calculated at 2 cubic meters per person per day, it can accommodate about 41,000 disaster victims. The water conservancy relations involve not only the three counties of Zhen, Dan, and Wu, but also the counties of Jin, Li, Yi, and Xi, all of which have great benefits.

(2) Dredging the Chishan Lake River Basin

The largest water source between the capital and Zhenjiang is no more than the west of the Maoshan Mountains, which is the Qinhuai River basin, and Chishan Lake in Jurong is its natural reservoir. In the Southern Tang Dynasty, it was one hundred and twenty kilometers in circumference, but now it is only more than forty li. There are forty-two weirs around the lake, no less than hundreds of thousands of mu of fields. Over the years, it has become easy to discharge and difficult to store. The Qinhuai River channel is silted up. Once mountain floods break out, the vast ocean goes straight down, and ten miles of villages are swept away, and the people are drowned. For example, the impact in 1920 of the Republic of China caused the capital to suffer particularly severely. In 1918 of the Republic of China, the former Jiangnan Water Conservancy Bureau had already measured and planned, but the construction has not been carried out. This province has strictly ordered the prohibition of reclamation and ordered the three relevant counties to collect labor to dredge. But the project is huge. According to the original plan, the length of the project has reached 95.86 kilometers, and the earthwork that should be excavated has been more than 7.89 million cubic meters. Now I am afraid it is not limited to this number. The people of the three counties have limited power and cannot be competent, so it has been delayed until now. Now it is planned to adopt the original plan and design in two items: 1. Water storage plan, (A) Building lake dikes, that is, dredging the river channel in the lake, and using the soil from the dredging to build lake dikes, combining dredging and building, without spending huge sums of money. (B) Returning the reclaimed land to the lake. The eleven weir areas around the lake, totaling about 8,800 mu, should be investigated to determine those who have reclaimed privately, and no compensation will be given. In addition, another circle will be purchased. (A) and (B) are carried out simultaneously, which can restore Chishan Lake to a smaller range of reservoir. 2. Water discharge plan, (C) Dredging the main stream of the Qinhuai River, starting from Sancha Town in Chishan Lake, bypassing the northern foot of Chishan Mountain to enter the Jinning Hushou, to the Northwest Village to meet the Lishui River, and then flowing northwest around the western foot of Fangshan Mountain, passing through Shangfangmen to the capital and entering the river. The most silted places are the section from Sancha Town to the Northwest Village and the section from Saihong Bridge to Xinhekou. This is the dredging route of the main stream. (D) Dredging the tributaries. Since the lake and the Huai River have been separated, it is planned to dredge the relevant tributaries. It is still not possible to plan to dredge to communicate the meridians and take into account the benefits of the upper and lower reaches. It should be dredged upstream of the three rivers in the north, south, and middle above the lake, and all should be directed to the lake to prevent flooding the plains. Below the lake, the Jurong River and Lishui should be dredged to be smooth and passable to reduce the disasters in Jurong and Lishui and increase the power of the Qinhuai River to clean the water. The above-mentioned projects are calculated according to the original estimated earthwork, and are already more than 7.89 million cubic meters. The current situation should be increased. Now it is planned to select the most important ones to handle. For the time being, this number is still used for calculation. Each cubic meter is estimated at one corner, about 880,000 yuan, plus about 700,000 yuan for purchasing land, building dikes, building dams, pumping water, and managing fees, totaling about 1.5 million yuan. This project is of great importance to the water conservancy of the three counties of Lishui, Jurong, and Jiangning. If it can be realized, it can accommodate 45,000 disaster workers and maintain it for three months.

(3) Dredging the Yili Canal and the Danjingli Caohe Canal

The west of the Maoshan Mountains is the Qinhuai River basin, as described in the previous section. The east of the Maoshan Mountains is the western upper reaches of the Taihu Lake basin, and its water flows east, except for storing water as Gehu Changdang, with the Yili Canal as the east-west trunk road. The Yili Canal starts from Dongtian in the west, passes through the Taihu Lake of Liyi people, and is about 80 kilometers long. The tributaries on both sides are divergent, and the farmland benefits from it. However, in recent years, it has also been in disrepair for a long time, and the knots have become shallow. The flood years cannot be discharged smoothly, resulting in clogging disasters. In drought years, it is impossible to draw back the water from Taihu Lake to provide relief. Therefore, this year's disaster is particularly severe and should be dredged section by section to benefit farmland, which will also be of great benefit to shipping. The Danjingli Caohe Canal is about 54 kilometers long and is one of the north-south trunk roads in the west of Taihu Lake, running through the three counties of Danjingli. Because the land is higher and the riverbed is shallow, it often flows dry every spring, and irrigation and shipping are both damaged. If it can be dredged, it can connect to the Yili Canal in the south and the Zhensu Canal in the north. On irrigation, it can achieve the effect of mutual adjustment, and on shipping, it can achieve the effect of Changtong. It is also an important plan to promote agricultural affairs, and it should not be delayed. The earth that needs to be excavated for dredging section by section of these two projects is about 4.5 million cubic meters. Each cubic meter is estimated at one corner, about 450,000 yuan, plus about 50,000 yuan for construction, filling, water drainage, management equipment, etc., totaling about 500,000 yuan, which can accommodate 25,000 disaster workers for three months.

(4) Subsidizing Liuhe, Liyang and Other Counties to Dredge Rivers and Open Ponds

This year's severe drought Jiangnan Zhenjiang, Danyang, Jintan, Yixing, Liyang, Lishui, Jurong, Gaochun, eight counties, and Jiangbei Liuhe, Jiangpu, Yizheng, Jiangdu four counties, suffered particularly severely. Therefore, the province will allocate additional funds to order the counties to use work-relief methods to dredge rivers and open ponds. It is planned to allocate a total of 1 million yuan, accommodating about 50,000 disaster workers for three months. (2nd)

Wuxi Land Price Declaration Begins 102

When Chairman Chiang Kai-shek convened administrative personnel from various provinces at a meeting in Nanchang in March of this year, he repeatedly admonished that the urban land tax should be planned and levied immediately. The Jiangsu Provincial Government believes that if the land price declaration is handled, the land price will be confirmed by the government, and the intangible society will increase a large amount of active funds, and the social economy will be developed, and the industry and commerce will be prosperous. When the method is prescribed, a resolution is made to implement it, and the county magistrates of Wuxi and Nantong are instructed to handle it carefully and complete it on schedule. After seeing the newspaper, Yang Hanxi, the chairman of the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce, Qian Jihou, the director of the County Asset Office, and Rong Zongjing, etc., the Wuxi compatriots in Shanghai, and Zhang Yioou Wang Kunlun and others, the compatriots in Beijing, all believed that the Jiangsu Province held a land price declaration, starting with Wuxi and Nantong counties, and Wuxi County city has not yet reached a completely autonomous period, and the land price declaration does not conform to the National Construction Outline. They immediately telegraphed Chairman Lin, President Wang, President Sun, Minister Kong, and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, as well as the Chairman of Jiangsu Province, Chen Guofu, etc., to ask them to cherish the local difficulties and issue an order to stop the land price declaration in Wuxi. Yesterday, Rong Zongjing and Yang Hanxi, etc., were specially instructed to understand this intention and assist in completing the declaration. Now it is learned that the land price declaration office should start household declarations from the 16th of last month in accordance with provincial regulations. Later, due to various reasons, the assistance committee decided to postpone it for one month and report it to the province for verification. A directive was received a few days ago that the household declaration should be handled in accordance with the prescribed time and should not be delayed. After the office was ordered, it has now started the declaration yesterday, starting with the city. It is heard that the scope of the declaration is limited to the jurisdiction of the first district of this county.

Fire in Dense Wave Sandbar Kills Four 105

At No. 103 Dense Wave Sandbar in Yongbo City, No. 14 small doorplate inside the Hanlin Residence, the owner Xie Chenshan is doing business in Dalian. He rented the house to Cai Changgen, Zhang Peihao, and Cai Changgen's relatives, the Ge Chen family mother and daughter. The house was a three-room, six-windowed building with high walls around it, and the construction was quite sturdy. Unexpectedly, at around 9 o'clock last night, due to carelessness with fire, a sudden conflagration broke out. By the time Ge Chen and her seventeen-year-old daughter, Ke Bei, who lived upstairs, heard the alarm and got up to escape, the stairs were already on fire, and they could not get downstairs, perishing in the fire. Cai Changgen's young son, Fuyin (currently eight years old), and young daughter, Fuqing, (currently eleven years old), were sleeping downstairs and could not be rescued, also being burned to death. After various fire brigades rushed to the scene to put out the fire, it took an hour to extinguish it. The entire house was burned down, resulting in a loss of over 10,000 taels of gold.

Thousands of Farmers in Northern Zhenhai Petition 106

More than 2,000 farmers from Tianyang Township, Haidian Township, Shishan Township, etc., in the third district of Zhenhai, due to severe drought and crop failure, gathered at the county government yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM to petition. The Xiepu Public Security Bureau was unable to stop them, and reported to the county government by telephone. After arriving at the county, the farmers demanded to be received by the county magistrate and presented three requests: (1) Exemption from land rent, (2) Postponement of last year's prepaid rent to offset next year's rent, (3) Exemption from grain tax. The county magistrate, Xu Yong, replied that the first two points needed to be discussed with the landlords, and the third point needed to be submitted to the province for approval. The farmers were dissatisfied with the county magistrate's reply and refused to leave the county government. Subsequently, members of the county party headquarters were sent to persuade them, but to no avail. As of 8:00 PM, the matter remained unresolved, and there was unrest in front of the county government. Later, the county magistrate telegraphed the Ningbo Garrison Command's First Regiment, which dispatched troops to suppress the situation. The farmers retreated to the City God Temple that night, and the petition event remains unresolved.

He Shangping Returned to Shanghai Yesterday 116

Drafting a Report on the Investigation of Sericulture in Shandong Province

According to the Huadong News Agency, He Shangping, Executive Committee Member of the Sericulture Improvement Association of the National Economic Council, went to Shandong last month to inspect sericulture and aims to improve sericulture in Shandong by next spring. He returned to Shanghai yesterday and drafted a very detailed report on the investigation of Shandong sericulture, and has established two improvement farms in the province. The full text of the report has been obtained by a reporter from the Huadong News Agency and is excerpted below:

Overview of Shandong Sericulture: Shandong sericulture is divided into mulberry sericulture and tussah sericulture. The mulberry sericulture area is most prosperous in Linqu, Mengyin, Xintai, Yidu, Boshan, Zhoucun, and other places along the Jiaoji Railway line. Tussah sericulture is centered on Yantai, Muping, and other places in eastern Shandong. Therefore, the route of this investigation is mainly along the Jiaoji Railway line, Zhoucun, Qingzhou, and various places in Yantai and Taocun.

Climate and Soil: The Shandong Peninsula is bounded by the Bohai Sea to the north and the Yellow Sea to the south. Except during the height of summer, the air is often foggy near Jiaozhou Bay and the air is relatively humid. Other places bordering the Bohai Bay to the north, from Weixian in the east to Zhangqiu in the west, have many mountains and smooth rivers. The climate is dry and mild during the spring and summer rainy seasons. The soil is fertile and free from waterlogging, making it more suitable for sericulture and mulberry planting than Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Since 1918, Chinese and foreign people and various sericulture agencies have repeatedly tried to raise European varieties and often achieved satisfactory results. Softening disease is rare, and the toxicity rate of microsporidia is also reduced. From this, it can be seen that Shandong sericulture can be said to be blessed by nature. At the time of the silk market's severe decline, if you want to save and reduce costs, Shandong is the only place to do it.

Mulberry Garden Situation: The variety of mulberry in Shandong is generally called Lu mulberry, among which there are yellow Lu mulberry, black Lu mulberry, etc. due to different skin colors. There is also a kind of Lu mulberry with a bud end leaf curl, shaped like a sheep's horn and chicken crown, which is widely planted in various places and is rich in yield, and it is valuable for preservation and reproduction. In recent years, various agencies have tried to plant Hu mulberry, but it has not been popularized. It is said that it is more prone to wilting disease than Lu mulberry and remains to be investigated. However, Hu mulberry is far less reliable than Lu mulberry in terms of cold resistance. Therefore, the future trend in Shandong is still to improve Lu mulberry as the main focus. There is no need to promote other varieties without considerable experimentation. As for the form of pruning, the original ones are mostly arbors, and there is no need to change them for a while. However, most of the cultivation methods are old-fashioned, and crops are often planted between mulberry trees, which is also the reason for the recent decline in the silk market and the farmers' economic hardship. Recently, it has been heard that in Lu Province, there are those who cut down mulberry trees and replant other crops, accounting for as much as one-third of the total, which is very frightening.

Silkworm Cocoon Situation: It has been found that the majority of silkworms in Lu Province are three-sleep silkworms. Although there are two types of three-sleep silkworms, yellow and white, yellow cocoons are still the majority. Their cocoon shape and cocoon color are very similar to Sichuan three-sleep cocoons. Their advantage is that the fiber is strong and the strength of the silk is strong, which is welcomed by the European market. Five years ago, the Golden Taishan brand raw silk produced by the Qingdao Suzuki Silk Factory was the best in the world, and it was this variety that was slightly improved and reeled in the cocoon factory. Later, the quality gradually declined, and the Silver Taishan brand came into being. Recently, the Golden and Silver Taishan brands have disappeared. This kind of high-quality fine silk is quite costly, and it is not worth the loss at today's silk prices. Recently, the four-sleep improved varieties used in Jiangnan have also been tried by the people, but the number is very small. In the future, Lu Province may also try to breed more European crossbreeds in order to improve quality rather than weight, in order to save the decline of the rural economy.

Silkworm Seed Manufacturing: Silkworm seeds are traditionally made by farmers themselves. Even the improved varieties produced by the Qingzhou Provincial Sericulture Experiment Farm are very small and do not help. Poor silkworm seeds and poor results cause farmers to lose more than they gain, which is also one of the important reasons for mulberry cutting. In other cases, such as in 1920 and 1921, silk merchants from Lu Province purchased four-sleep improved varieties from Jiangnan and distributed them around Zhoucun, and the results were good. The number of white cocoons of Xin Yuan Zhe Gui that are now scattered among the people is its inheritance. At the same time, the Japanese reeling silk in Qingdao also distributed improved varieties to Qingzhou, Zhoucun, and other places, but they were only a flash in the pan.

Old Method of Drying Cocoons: Silk factories still use the old method of drying cocoons, and farmers are often unwilling to sell them because the cocoon prices are too low, and they pickle the cocoons with salt. It is unknown how many silkworm cocoons have been ruined in this way. Therefore, if you want to improve Lu silk, and establish public cocoon drying, it is a matter of urgency. According to He Shangping yesterday, when he spoke to the Huadong News Agency reporter who visited him, he said that after personally inspecting the sericulture industry in Shandong Province, he deeply felt that Shandong Province is the most suitable area in China for planting mulberry trees and raising silkworms, because the soil and climate are more suitable than those in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Therefore, he has now set up two autumn cocoon guidance centers in Linqu and Yidu, and distributed 200 sheets of improved varieties. During the autumn silkworm season, he will first conduct a trial experiment, and next spring, he will persuade people in the province to raise improved varieties to achieve improvement. As for the spring silkworms in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, Zhejiang has 600,000 sheets, each sheet has about 35 jin of fresh cocoons, Jiangsu has 25 jin, and Sichuan has about 22 jin. Although the harvest cannot be said to be abundant, it cannot be said to be poor. The autumn silkworms have been distributed, and the early ones have produced two-sleep, and the late autumn silkworms will also be distributed within the next few days. As for the overseas sales agency proposed by Chu Huiseng, the leader of the silk business community, the association is very supportive in principle, but the association is urgently needed to enrich the silk production step by step, so it is a pity that it cannot take care of it at the same time.

Zhejiang and Anhui Green Tea Sales are Slow 117

Pingshui Tea Costs 60 Yuan Per Load, Not Enough to Cover Costs

Wuyuan Tea, More Than 20,000 Boxes, is Difficult to Ship to Shanghai Due to Shallow Water

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the production and sales of Pingshui green tea in Zhejiang, and Tunxi and Wuyuan green tea in Anhui this year are as follows:

Low Price of Pingshui Green Tea: Pingshui Town in Zhejiang is the central area of the green tea market in Shaoxing County. The types produced are divided into silkworm eye, ant eye, butterfly eye, mosquito eye, etc., collectively known as Pingshui tea. They are packed into boxes and sold abroad, with the United States accounting for the most sales, followed by Russia and France. In its heyday, the annual sales volume was more than 500,000 boxes. In the past ten years, the European and American markets have been encroached upon by Indian and Ceylon tea. According to the statistics of the foreign tea industry association, it has dropped to 180,000 boxes. This year, the export of Chinese tea is even worse than before. Pingshui green tea is no exception. Last year, the price of tea was about 70 yuan per load, but this year it has fallen by about 10 yuan, to only about 60 yuan. Tea merchants cannot even cover their principal, and are all very frustrated. In the blink of an eye, the Mid-Autumn Festival is approaching, and the financial situation is extremely tight. It is not easy to improve sales and market prices.

New Tea in Wuyuan is Difficult to Transport Due to River Drying: In addition to specializing in foreign-style Zhenmei and Dabang for sale to Europe and the United States, the leftover tea scraps from Wuyuan County, Anhui Province, are transported to various tea shops in China for domestic consumption. This year, due to poor production, the tea shops have given priority to purchasing in order to transport them to Shanghai for sale. However, due to severe drought, the rivers have dried up, and the navigation of the Rao River and Huijiang River has been blocked. All the shops are hoarding tea in the production area, waiting for the water to start shipping. At the current market price, there is no big profit to be made, but prolonged delay will only consume interest. Therefore, the tea merchants are very anxious. According to the Tea Industry Association, there are about 20,000 boxes of tea that have been stranded in the production area. However, it is difficult to predict when these boxes of tea can be transported to Shanghai because there is no water to sail the boats.

China Merchants Bureau Improves Water and Land Combined Transport on All Routes 121

Pinghan Railway Scheduled to be Implemented on the 15th

To be Handled Concurrently with Private Sanbei and Others

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, after the state-owned China Merchants Bureau contracted the national railway water and land combined transport, it carried out improvements to the combined transport on the Longhai Railway and other routes. As for the improved combined transport measures for the Jiaoji Railway, it was decided to implement them from September 1. Regardless of whether the goods are transported from various stations to various ports, or from various ports to various stations, the freight will be calculated in accordance with the combined transport price list, and one ticket will be directly available. All freight can be paid in advance or on delivery. Advance payment must be paid in full at the time of shipment, and payment on delivery must be paid at the place of arrival. All procedures for customs duties at Jiaohai Customs and the inspection bureau of the port authority can also be handled by the two bureaus on behalf of the merchants, and the merchants do not need to take care of them in Qingdao. As for all the measures for the water and land combined transport on the Pinghan Railway, they are all ready and it has been decided to implement them simultaneously with the private Sanbei Shipping Company and the Ning Shao Shipping Company. Mr. Gu, seeing the severity of the disaster in his hometown, was moved with compassion and purchased 500 shi of brown rice in Shanghai, which was shipped to Xia on the last month and entrusted to someone to start by investigating the poorest and poorest farmers. Once the procedures are completed, all the relief rice will be distributed. The disaster victims in the five districts of Ningyi are waiting to be fed. They will get a great deal from this benevolent relief rice. However, there is more than one wealthy merchant from Haining living in Shanghai (Mr. Gu's ancestral home is Haiyan, and he has lived in Xiashi Town, Haining for generations). There should be those who rise up in response and do not let Mr. Gu monopolize the beauty of the moment.

Page 13

Xiang Kangyuan Returns from an Inspection Tour of Southeast Asia 123

He Speaks of the Miserable and Painful Impressions Gathered Along the Way

Young Overseas Chinese in Siam Do Not Recognize Their Motherland

The Domestic Market is Entirely Plundered by Japanese Goods

According to the Shen Shi News Agency, Mr. Xiang Kangyuan, a prominent industrialist, departed two months ago for Southeast Asia to inspect industrial and commercial activities, as well as the economic situation of overseas Chinese. Over the course of two months, he visited Malaya, Siam, Burma, Annam, Singapore, Penang, and other places, gaining profound impressions. Mr. Xiang has now completed his inspection and returned, arriving in Shanghai the day before yesterday. Yesterday, a reporter from the Shen Shi News Agency made a special visit to interview him, and he detailed the painful impressions he gained during his trip regarding the overseas Chinese in various regions, as well as the crisis facing Chinese goods in Southeast Asia. The details are recorded as follows:

Painful Impressions from Southeast Asia – According to Mr. Xiang, of all the places I

visited in Southeast Asia, Siam left the deepest impression. When I arrived in that port and before I even disembarked, I was subjected to unreasonable and harsh questioning and inspection by customs officials. This situation is especially difficult for Chinese people, and there is no legal recourse. This is because our country has not sent a consul to the area, and overseas Chinese are largely at the mercy of their whims, with the possibility of being arbitrarily expelled or imprisoned. I once met a customs official on a boat who, because his appearance did not resemble that of a Siamese, was questioned. He truthfully stated that his father was Chinese and his mother was Siamese. Because his father was unrighteous, he did not want to follow his father but followed his mother, and he obtained his current customs official position in Siam thanks to his mother's Siamese nationality. When asked about the situation in China, he said that China was a small and insignificant country, with no products to export, and relied on Siamese food (namely, what we Chinese call coarse rice) for survival. The Chinese population is increasing, but because their own country cannot accommodate them, they migrate to Siam every year. Hearing his words, I was speechless. For a descendant of overseas Chinese to utter such words, the shallowness and alienation of their impression of their ancestral country is evident, which is truly heartbreaking.

Overseas Chinese Commerce is Declining Rapidly – Historically, commerce in Southeast Asia was pioneered and created by overseas Chinese from our country. After more than four hundred years of arduous operation, the domestic goods currently sold are still old-fashioned products from the 18th century. This is a world apart from the latest Western mechanical products. Furthermore, forty years ago, the commercial industry of overseas Chinese was gradually seized by British and Dutch Western goods. In recent times, the Japanese have used dumping policies to compete with British and Dutch goods, and within only twenty years, the Western goods business market has been completely seized by Japanese goods. Currently, Japanese goods account for a staggering 95% of Siam's imports. However, according to the Siamese Immigration Bureau, there are only 435 Japanese immigrants in Siam, 2,700 Europeans, 4 million Chinese, and 2 million of mixed Chinese-Siamese descent. The Japanese immigrants have operated in Siam for less than twenty years, with a population of less than 500, yet they have been able to control the country's economy. Our country has operated in Siam for 400 years, with a population of 6 million, but we are now surpassed by those who came later, which is truly shameful.

Japanese Goods Sell Well in Malaya, etc. – The situation in other places such as the Malayan Islands, Annam, Burma, and Singapore is largely the same as described above. The dumping of Japanese goods is unbelievable. For example, in Kuala Lumpur, Japanese undershirts sell for only 40 cents per dozen, light bulbs for only 2.5 cents each, and silk cheongsam fabric for only 70 cents per piece. No other country in the world could compete with them. However, according to the overseas Chinese compatriots in the area, as long as there are domestic Chinese goods available, they are willing to buy them even if the prices are twice as high. This shows the passion and deep love of overseas Chinese for their motherland. If the people of our country can pay attention to promotion, there may be a way to salvage the situation.

Overseas Chinese in Various Regions Sell Domestic Products – Mr. Xiang continued, "Overseas Chinese in various regions have often told me that they are very willing to promote domestic products and are happy to purchase them. However, in the past, when they priced or inquired about prices in China, the replies they received often did not address their questions, or they received no response at all. Sometimes orders were not delivered on time, the goods often did not match the original samples, and the quantities were short. No reasons were given for these problems, or if there were reports, they would arrive only after a month or half a month. These various reasons have caused even the most enthusiastic overseas Chinese to gradually become discouraged. This situation is very regrettable and needs to be urgently remedied."

The Promotion of Domestic Goods Should Be Carried Out Quickly – Currently, the older overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia still have a deep understanding of their motherland. However, the younger generation is mostly fond of using foreign goods and has a vague and uncaring impression of their ancestral country. Therefore, if domestic goods are not promoted and developed at this time, in a few years, when the older generation passes away and the younger generation lacks a concept of their motherland, it will be even more difficult to promote domestic goods. If our country does not pay attention to the Southeast Asian market in the next five or ten years, I fear that trade in Southeast Asia will never be recovered by us. I hope that our government and people will pay attention to this and actively develop it.

Overseas Chinese Business Delegations Return to China for Inspection – Mr. Xiang finally said that the decline in the promotion of domestic products by overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia and the suffering of overseas Chinese abroad is largely due to the lack of close contact between overseas Chinese and their home country, which has created a detached phenomenon. The difficulties and inconveniences faced in Annam, Siam, and Malaya make the overseas Chinese in these areas eager for the government to send consuls to take charge as soon as possible. Furthermore, the overseas Chinese in various places feel that they do not have a clear understanding of the recent situation in their motherland, including the progress of our country's politics, economy, and industry and commerce. Therefore, I have strongly encouraged them to return to China to conduct inspections in order to understand the situation and plan for joint development. Many overseas Chinese have expressed their willingness. Around the end of this year, overseas Chinese from Singapore, Siam, Malaya, and other places will come to Shanghai to inspect the actual situation in China and the progress of industry and commerce in order to jointly seek overseas development.

Fishing Boats are Prohibited from Anchoring and Netting Near Submarine Cables 125

To Avoid Damaging the Cables and Disrupting Communications

Joint Proclamation by the Social Affairs Bureau and the Public Utilities Bureau

The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau received instructions from the Ministry of Industry, approving a communication from the Ministry of Transportation, stating that the submarine cable from Wusong to Yantai has recently been frequently disrupted, mostly due to fishing boats anchoring and netting. Yesterday, it issued orders to the city's fishing organizations and, together with the Public Utilities Bureau, issued the following joint proclamation: The Social Affairs Bureau has received instructions from the Ministry of Industry, approving a communication from the Ministry of Transportation, stating that the submarine cables from Wusong to Yantai, Yantai to Dagu, and Qingdao to Sasebo are crucial for north-south communication and communication between China and Japan. In recent months, they have been frequently disrupted, which not only greatly affects telecommunications but also causes significant losses due to years of repairs. Repeated reports indicate that the cause of the damage is mostly due to fishing boats anchoring or netting. It is imperative to strictly prohibit fishing boats from anchoring or dropping fishing gear near the submarine cables to avoid damaging them and maintain telecommunications. The original attachments are included, ordering immediate compliance and proclamation to inform fishermen to avoid such actions. Upon receiving these instructions, the Social Affairs Bureau has already issued orders to the Shanghai Fishermen's Association and the Shanghai Fishing Vessel Industry Association to instruct fishing vessel companies to comply. Hereafter, when fishing vessels go to sea, they must not anchor or drop fishing gear near the submarine cables to avoid damaging them. This joint proclamation by the Social Affairs Bureau, etc., is for all fishing vessels to comply with. This proclamation is issued on September 1, the 23rd year of the Republic of China, by Wu Xingya, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, and Xu Peihuang, Director of the Public Utilities Bureau.

This Year's Grain Transportation on Both Railways is Exceptionally High 127

This year, the transportation of grain (wheat and rice) on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways has been exceptionally high. According to investigations, since May of this year, the Beijing-Shanghai Railway has been transporting wheat (from Shandong and Henan provinces) at a rate of 150 to 160 cars per day. By the end of this month, approximately 14,500 cars will have been transported. On the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, at least 20 rice cars are loaded at Maigeng Road and Rihui Port and transported to the Shiqiao and Gongchenqiao and Zhakou stations every day. Other cargo volumes have decreased compared to previous years.

Guichi County Sends Another Telegram to Xinwei Relief Association for Disaster Relief 132

280,000 Disaster Victims are Starving

Yesterday, the Xinwei Relief Association of the Renji Charity Hall in Shanghai received another telegram from Guichi County, Anhui Province, requesting disaster relief to save lives. The original telegram is recorded below: "To the Xinwei Relief Association of the Shanghai Renji Hall, We humbly report that Guichi County is suffering from a severe drought, and the lives of the people are in danger. Previously, various local institutions and legal entities jointly telegraphed to request urgent relief to provide food for the people, which we believe has been acknowledged. Since the autumn equinox, it has still not rained, and the drought has become even more severe, causing widespread panic. Our association has been organized in accordance with the provincial government's order, called the Drought Relief, but the actual disaster has already occurred and cannot be remedied. In addition to opening granaries and selling grain at reduced prices to temporarily alleviate the current situation, there is not much grain in storage, and it will be difficult to sustain. Therefore, we have to find ways to provide relief to save the disaster victims and maintain order. It has been found that since the Dragon Boat Festival, there has been no rain in Guichi County, and the drought has been severe. Not only are the fields dry and the land cracked, and the seedlings withered and died, but also the ponds, wells, streams, and rivers have all dried up. Not only are the waterwheels exhausted, but the people also have no water to drink. Such an unusual drought has not been heard of in a hundred years. Since the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, the county has been exhausting the supply of military service, followed by the ravages of bandits, and then the great flood of the twentieth year. Natural and man-made disasters have come one after another. Last year's autumn harvest was also affected by drought in high-lying areas and flooding in low-lying areas. The local vitality has long been injured, and the rural economy has been bankrupted. This year, there is an even greater drought. 280,000 lives are at stake, as if hanging upside down. Not only is there no surplus seed, but people are waiting for death. The situation is unbearable. The current situation is dire, and the future is unimaginable. We are local people and feel the pain deeply, but we have no way to provide relief. Therefore, we send a telegram to appeal, admiring your association's compassion and concern. We hope that you will generously grant relief and save the disaster victims, which will not only be appreciated by the local people but will also be an immeasurable merit. With urgent words, we are extremely fearful. The Guichi County Drought Relief Committee bows."

Nine Russian Fugitives Arrested 134

One Woman Among Them is a U.S. Citizen

Russia Requests Extradition; We Are Considering Carefully

A week ago, the Shanghai Municipal Government received an official document from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs stating that, according to a notification from the Russian Minister to China, Bogomolov, nine Russian fugitives, who had committed murder in Vladivostok, Russia, had secretly come to Shanghai aboard a Russian cargo ship. The Russian Minister is currently discussing extradition with our foreign affairs authorities. As a matter of sovereignty, we will handle this matter carefully.
